 Guru Purnima has special significance in Hinduism
 hinduon main guru kaa sarvshereshth sthaan he
 Even the status of the Guru is above that of God because it is the Guru who leads us to the right path by ridding us from the darkness of ignorance
 yahi vajah he ki desh bhar main guru poornima kaa utsav dhoomdhaam se manaaya jaataa he
 It is believed that on this day Adiguru, the author of the Mahabharata and the interpreter of the four Vedas, Maharishi Krishna Dvaipayan Vyas i
e
 Maharishi Veda Vyas (ved Vyas) was born
 ve sanskrit ke mahaan vidwaan the
 An epic like Mahabharat is given by him
 isi ke 18wein adhyay main bhagwaan shri krishna gita kaa upadesh dete hai
 The author of all 18 Puranas is also considered to be Maharishi Ved Vyasa
 vedon ko vibhajit karne kaa shrey bhi inhen ko diya jaataa he
 For this reason, he was named Ved Vyas
 vedavyas ji ko aadiguru bhi kaha jaataa he isliye guru poornima ko vyas poornima (vyas Purnima) ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he
 On the day of Guru Purnima, there is a law to worship the Guru
 is baar guru poornima ke din chandra grahan (lunar Eclipse) bhi he
 Maharishi Parashar could not live without being attracted to Satyavati
 unhone satyavati se unhone nadi paar karwaane kii guzarish kii
 Satyavati invited him to sit in his boat
 naav main baithne ke baad parashar rishi ne satyavati ke saamne pranay nivedan kiya, jise satyavati ne sashart sweekaar kiya
 Parashar wanted to have intercourse with the sage, Satyavati, before Satyavati placed three conditions before him
 satyavati kii pehali shart thi ki unhen sambhog karte hue koi bhi jeev naa dekh paae

 The cloud of smoke produced by burning straw in Punjab makes it difficult for people to breathe in the National Capital Region (NCR) and large parts of North India every year
 ab punjab ne ek mahatvakankshi kaarykram kaa sahaara liya he, taaki har saal dhan kii fasal se bachane vaali kareeb 2 karod ton paraali ko surakshit tareeke se khapaaya ja sake
 The state government has tied up with Chennai-based solid waste management firm Nivea Engineers Private Limited using 'zero Residue Technology' to produce problematic straw or straw with high-energy carbon-rich fuel (CEF), bricks and paver blocks Will change to yadi company or punjab ke nivesh protsaahan beuro ke bich hue emoyu ke mutabik kaam hua, to rajya ke kisaanon ko khet taiyaar karne ke liye dhan kii paraali ko jalaane kii jarurat nahin hogi
 The farmers burn the straw to harvest the rabi crop
 nive main senior diarector es
 K
 sivakumar kehete hai, ''company aisi 100 ikaayiyon kaa nirmaan karegi jahaan puure rajya se ikattha kii gai dhan kii paraali kii processing kii jaaegi or ise rajya main bane kareeb 400 kendron main rakhaa jayega
 "we will use a new carbonization-devolating process, for which patents have been applied in 148 countries including India, the European Union and North America," he explains
 '' sivakumar ne kaha ki nive pehle se hi safaltaapurvak is takanic kaa istemaal chennai main nagar nigam ke thos kachare (emesdblyoo) ko siief eendhan main badalane main kar rahi he
 Rakesh Kumar Verma, head of the Punjab Investment Bureau, says Nivea has launched Rs 10,000 crore to launch its unique agri-residue management system
 ke nivesh kaa vachan diya he
 This system will start working 10 months from now
 sivakumar or unke sahyogiyon ke mutabik, aktubar 2018 kii fasal se pehle har kisaan or kisaan sanghathan isse jud jaaen, yah yojana he
 Nivea will set up a farmer hotline running around the clock for 24 hours and will purchase parali according to the crop cycle of Malwa, Doaba and Majha areas
 is upkram se kareeb 30,000 logon ko rojgaar milegaa, kyonki nive ke kaamkaaj main masini nikasi, kataai, sukhaane or paraali kaa ga-r bana use cluster binduon tak pahunchane ke liye shramik chahie honge
 Each cluster point will have a capacity to hold about 50,000 tonnes of straw
 aise prayek centre kaa nirmaan saat acre jameen main kiya jayega or iske liye jameen sthaneey panchayat yaa logon se lij par lee jaaegi
 However, this will be a big challenge as Nivea will get barely a month to remove all 20 million tonnes of straw from the fields so that it can be sown for the Rabi crop in time
 iske liye company prati acre maamuli 'yujar charge' legi

 prati acre ho saktaa he

 ) kahaan se aegi? is par sivakumar kehete hai, ''singapore or honkong ke nijee niveshkon ke ek consorcium kii taraf se paisa aayega, jo teesri duniya kii harith yojanaon main nivesh karne ke icchhuk hai
 "nivea has proposed to give 50 per cent stake to such investors and a representative of the company believes that" money is not a big problem
 ''philhal jin technology kaa istemaal kiya gaya he, unamem shaharon ke thos kachare ko lo caloriffic vailu vaale ardf (rifyus-dirivd ful) main badla jaataa he or iskaa bada hissaa kachare ke dher main badal jaataa he
 But Nivea's proprietary technology produces cefs with calorific values of 4,000 to 5,000 kcal per kilogram
 agar tulanaatmak rup se dekhen to zyaadaatar thermal power plant main jis koyale kaa istemaal hota he uski caloriffic vailu sirf 2,500 hoti he or uskaa 40 fisadi hissaa raakh ke rup main baahar aata he
 Cement plants are also reluctantly used by rdfs, while carbon-rich fuels are in great demand, as they would be used in cement, iron and steel, sugarcane, paper, thermal power plants and in all areas such as methanol or ethanol production
 is
 mukhyamantri amarinder singh bhi ise anoothaa harith vikalp maanate hue is venture kaa samarthan kar rahe hai, lekin rajya ke prashasnic halake main ise lekar abhi bhi kuch andeh he
 Many are skeptical of Nivea's ability to operate on such a large scale, as its current asset value is just Rs 32 crore
 he or vah punjab main vishalkay 10,000 karod ke upkram par kaam karne kii baat kar rahi he
 The State Investment Bureau is saying that it is fully vigilant in this matter, but Verma says that it has no financial implications for the state government, as it is only giving the company the facility to start operations in Punjab
 unhone kaha ki ''project se jo naukariyaan paidaa hongi, vah ek khushi dene vaale bonus kii tarah hongi
 "if all goes well, by next season, Punjab's contribution in preparing the cloud of smog in Delhi may be zero
" raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ne aaj nyaayamurti pi sadashivam ko desh ke 40wein pradhan nyaayadhish ke taur par shapath dilaai
 Justice Sadasivam (64) replaces Justice Altamas Kabir, who served as Chief Justice for nine months
 raashtrapati bhawan ke darbar haul main yojit ek sankshipt samaaroh main nyaayamurti sadashivam ne ishwar ke naam par shapath lee

 agast, 2007 main nyaayamurti sadashivam ko supreme court kaa nyaayadhish banaaya gaya tha or vah pradhan nyaayadhish ke pad par 26 april, 2014 tak karyrat rahenge
 Like Justice Altamas Kabir, Justice Sadasivam is also opposed to the abolition of the existing collegium system for appointment of judges of the Supreme Court and High Court
 iske saath hi unhone sweekaar kiya he ki colegium vyavastha main kamiyaan hai or paardarshita sunishchit karne ke liye prayaas kiye ja sakate hai
 Justice Sadasivam was born on April 27, 1949
 unhone july, 1973 main madras main bataur vakil panjikaran karavaaya or janvari, 1996 main madras ucch nyaayalay ke sthai nyaayadhish ke rup main niyukt hue
 He was then transferred to the Punjab and Haryana High Court in April 2007
 pradhan nyaayadhish ke taur par apni yojana ke bare main unhone guuruuvaar ko kaha tha, maamalon ke niptaare main vilamb ek bada mudda he
 This problem can be overcome by increasing the quality and quantity of justice

 Bhikhu Parekh It is often forgotten how huge the achievements of Mahatma Gandhi were
 unki 150veen jayanti ke maukey par unhen yaad karnaa acha hoga
 He was the first Indian to bring India to the global map and also the only Indian to be known worldwide
 ve pehle bhartiya the jinhone bharat se pehle bharat ke baahar apni rajnatik chhap chodi
 He has been the greatest leader in the history of India, mobilizing people behind him, who brought millions of men and especially women into public life
 ek-chauthai sadi tak bhartiya raajnneeti main unka itnaa bolbalaa rahaa ki jisane bhi unki naaraazgi mol lee, usne rajnatik aatmahatya kii
 He was the only Indian, but truly, leader of the world who touched life on many different levels and each of them had something to say about it, whether it was health, cleanliness, childbearing
 -ability, morality, sexuality, religion, economy or top-class politics
 aazaadee ke vakt, jiske liye ve ji-jaan se lade the, chautarafa faili hinsa se gandhi itane dukhi the ki unhone rashtriya dhvaj fahraane se or sandesh tak dene se inkaar kar diya
 He refused to take any political position for himself and spent the last two years of his life healing the wounds of communal violence
 yahaan tak ki jab unke sharir main sahane kii takat nahin bachi, tab bhi unhone upwas kiye, noakhli ke gaanvon kii patharilii sadakon par akele chale or peediton se guzarish kii ki ve dayalutaa or kshamaa dikhaaen
 Although his life was in danger, he flatly refused to take security and not only challenged his critics to the worst, but even to the feast, one of which he did
 haalanki, gandhi kii apni simaaen thim, par anek kshetron main ve behad prerak or shikshaprad the or yahi unhen 20veen sadi ke mahanatam logon main se ek banaata he
 Gandhi suffered repression and injustice in most of his adult life
 dakshin africa main first class main safar kii jurrat karne kii vajah se ek sard raat unhen train se nikaalkar baahar phenk diya gaya, gaali-galouj karte hue conductor ne unhen coach se neeche patake diya or vah to ganimat thi ki saathi musafiron ne unhen bachaa liya
 To pretend to pass in front of President Krueger's house in Pretoria, the concierge kicked him and dropped him into the groove
 transwaal main unhen 1900 ke registration kanoon kaa virodh karne kii vajah se giraftaar kar liya gaya or aam mujarimon ke saath jail kii kothri main rakhaa gaya, jo unki taraf yon ishaare or unki maujuudagi main bhaddi harakatein karte the
 In Durban, a racist white mob hurled stones at them and were beaten to such an extent that they had to take shelter in a nearby police station to save their lives, and later could go out in disguise as policemen
 gandhi ne apane in or aise hi duusare anubhavon par gaharaai se soch-vichaar kiya or poocha ki yah sara daman tathaa atyaachaar kyon hua or usamen peedit kii kya bhoomika thi
 They came to the conclusion that the victims of Daman were not innocent at all
 darasal, apane daman main unki mileebhagat thi
 The British ruled India with the help of Indians
 jaliyanvaala baag narsanhaar main bhartiya sainikon ne hi apane saathi bharatiyon par goliyaan chalaayin
 Gandhi went even further and argued that all this strength was finally achieved only with the help of the victim, without which they would have been hollow
 chunki saadhaaran aadamiyon or auraton ke bheetar is kism kii takat maujuud thi, isliye jarurat is baat kii thi ki ve apni aazaadee kii khatir yah takat dikhaaen or apane maalikon ko sahyog dene se inkaar karen
 Most of them were unable to do so due to fear or nervousness
 dakshin africa main bharatiyon ko jhidakate hue gandhi ne kaha ki jo khud keedon-makodon kii tarah vyavhaar karte hai, unhen kuchle jane par dusron ko dosha nahin dena chahie
 In another context, he also asked the Indians to learn to 'revolt against themselves'
 gandhi ke liye saahas aatm-sammaan se bandhaa tha or mahaan maanviya gun tha
 His concern was how to awaken the self-esteem of the victims of injustice
 jaisaa ki nehru ne kaha tha, unka sabase bada yogadan yah tha ki unhone bharat ko jakade hue dar kii chadar hataa di or uske bhaybheet or sankochi logon ko takat di
 Another area in which Gandhi spoke deep is related to his practice of non-violence
 unke tain ise galat samajha gaya tha ki keval nuksaan na pahunchaana hi ahimsa he
 If an animal is dying of an incurable disease and has only a few hours of life left, then it is an act of love to end its life by injecting life-threatening injections
 isamen hinsa he, par yah hinsak krity nahin he
 As Gandhi once said, the correct English translation of non-violence is not 'non-violence' but 'compassion' or 'love'
 kai duusare pahaluon main bhi gandhi ne ahimsa kii avadharana ko vistaar or gaharaai di
 Loss in the Indian tradition is defined in a way that includes not only physical harm but also psychological, moral and other forms of suffering or affliction
 gandhi ne is vyapak paribhaasha ko na keval sweekaar kiya balki iskaa vistaar bhi kiya
 In his opinion, one can harm or kill someone by firing bullets or depriving him of basic necessities of life for a long time
 chaahe koi 'ek jatke main' maare yaa 'thodaa-thodaa karke', nateeja vahi hota he or isliye usamen shaamil vyakti hinsa kaa doshi he
 Disrespecting, degrading or humiliating others, hurting self-esteem, uttering harsh words, imposing tough judgments, anger and mental cruelty are also forms of violence
 gandhi kaa ahimsa kaa vichaar satyagrah ke aacharan par aadhaarit tha, jisamen duusare ko khud apni pidaa ke jariye badla jaataa he
 He called it 'tearing of the soul'
 satyagrahi jise satya yaa nyaaysangat maang samajhataa he, uske aadhaar par apana rukh tay karata he, par saath hi apane sangharsh kii roshni main apane vichaaron ko badalane kii sambhaavna ko bhi khulaa rakhata he
 He aroused the superior tendencies of his adversary, groped his conscience, opened his heart and mind and sought his cooperation in the search and attainment of a just solution
 haalanki, gandhi bahut dharmik vyakti the, ve kisi kattarpanthi yaa dharmaandh vyakti se sabase zyada alag bhi the
 This was because he firmly believed that no religion is perfect and he must confine himself to the test of human logic and experience
 yah kabhi purna isliye nahin ho saktaa kyonki isaki abhivyakti ek khaas bhashaa main, itihaas ke khaas padaav par hui or uski tarah-tarah kii vyakhyaayein kii ja sakati hai
 Since this is so, every religion deserves respect
 saath hi, vah dusron se bhi bahut kuch sikh saktaa he or isliye duusare dharmon ke saath use vinamrata se pesh aana chahie
 Gandhi himself, while presenting a great example of this, borrowed openly from other religions, especially from Christianity, and blended it beautifully into Hinduism
 gandhi kaa maardarshak siddhant yah tha ki udaatt vichaaron ko sabhi dishaao se apane paas aane do
 He wanted to live in a house with walls for his protection, but with his windows open so that fresh thoughts would come
 gahare arth main gandhi bahusaanskrithikta yaa samskritiyon ke saath rachanaatmak samvaad ke pehle siddhantkaar or sadhak the
 His way of understanding the nature of religion is safe from fundamentalism and is very relevant to our difficult world
 gandhi kaa rajnatik netritv kaa vichaar bhi itnaa hi lubhaavna or prerak he
 As a leader of the national movement, he was very cautious about what to expect from the leader and the limits of his strength
 jab unhen laga ki unka asahyog andolan galat disha main chalaa gaya or hinsak ho uthaa he, tab unhone ise himalay jaisi baari bhul bataaya or waapas le liya
 It is difficult to find any other leader in history who has openly admitted his mistake and tried to improve
 sampradayik hinsa ko lekar bhi gandhi aisa hi sochate the, khaskar 1946 or 1948 ke bich
 He felt that he might not have paid enough attention to it
 chote se chote galat faisle ke liye khud ko takalif dene vaale shakchas hone ke naate gandhi ne isaki nijee jimmedaari lee or hinsa ke khilaaf apni ladaai main apni jaan tak jhonk di
 As a leader, he felt that it was his duty not to step too far ahead of his colleagues, let alone go against his thoughtful decision
 yah bhi ek vajah thi ki ve desh ke bantwaare ke khilaaf 'aamaran anshan' ke apane aadhe-adhure vaade par aage nahin bade, khaskar tab jab unke takreeban tamaam varisht saathi bantwaare ko sweekaar kar chuke the
 Gandhi had his limitations
 jaisaa ki nehru ne lord mountbayton se kaha tha, gandhi itane manushya the ki sant nahin ho sakate the
 His views on celibacy tested faith and his idea of sexuality as an animalistic impulse ignores its rich moral and emotional potential
 ahimsa kii param shakti main unka vishwaas bholaa-bhaalaa tha
 As Martin Buber and others have pointed out, the Nazis would have dealt with Gandhi even before he took his first step towards Satyagraha
 unhen buraai kii fitrat or gaharaai ke bare main simit samaj thi or uski maujuudagi se ve hakkaa-bakka mahasoos karte the
 Despite these and similar personal and philosophical limitations, Gandhi's ideas have the potential to show us the way
 unke jivan main, jise unhone apana sandesh kaha tha, durlabh gaharaai or bhavyata thi
 On his 150th birth anniversary, we should study his thoughts with gratitude and take inspiration from whatever deep things we find relevant and trustworthy
